UGosiame Thamara Sithole , 37 , ubeleke aba bantwana balishumi ( decuplets ngesiNgesi ) kwisibhedlele sasePitoli ngokuhlwa kwangoMvulo , utshilo umyeni wakhe uTeboho Tsotetsi .
UGosiame Thamara Sithole nomyeni wakhe uTeboho Tsotetsi UMFANEKISO : Thobile Mathonsi / African News Agency ( ANA )
UTsotetsi uthi uSithole , osuka kwilokishi yaseTembisa Ekurhuleni , ubeleke amakhwenkwe asixhenxe namantombazana amathathu emva kokusetyenziswa kwesikere .
" Ebeneenyanga ezisixhenxe neentsuku ezisixhenxe ekhulelwe .
Ndineemvakalelo , " utshilo uTsotetsi , ongaphangeliyo .
USithole , okwanamawele aneminyaka emithandathu , uxelele iPretoria News kwinyanga ephelileyo ukuba wayengayikholelwa ekuqaleni kwalo nyaka xa wayexelelwa ngoogqirha ukuba ukhulelwe abantwana abathandathu ( sextuplets ) , phambi kokuba olunye upopolo luveze ukuba unabantwana abasibhozo ( octuplets ) .
Abanye ababini zange babhaqwe ekuqaleni kuba babekumbhobho ongalunganga , ngokokutsho kukaSithole .
USithole , ongumanejala evenkileni , uthi kwakumothusile ukukhulelwa olu hlobo .
Uthi kwakunzima ekuqaleni , egula .
Ukwathe khange akunyangele ukukhulelwa .
UNjingalwazi Dini Mawela , isekela ntloko kwisikolo sezobugqirha eSefako Makgatho Health Sciences University , uthi imeko kaSithole inqabile kwaye ivame ukubangelwa lunyango lokufuna ukukhulelwa .
Aba bantwana baza kugqiba ezi nyanga zizayo kwizixhobo zokukhulisa abantwana ngenxa yokuba bebekhulelwe " ngomngcipheko ophezulu , " utshilo uMawela .
Ndenza isiqinisekiso sokuba olu phando nalo msebenzi ujongene nendlela apho abalinganiswa ababhinqileyo abathi bazotywa ngayo kwincwadi zedrama ngokubhekisele kwisini sabo sabosobufazi , wenziwe ndim .
Apho ndisokusebenziso aphando lwabanye ababhali , ndizokucaphula ukuba ndisebenzisa amagama omnye umbhali .
Kolu phando bekujongwane nendlela apho ababhali abasini sobuduna kwakunye nabo babhinqileyo abathi babazobe ngayo abalinganiswa abayintloko , abangamabhiqa kwiincwadi zabo zedrama zolwimi lwesiXhosa .
Umphandi ukhokelwe yinto yokuba kukho ingxaki kwindlela amabali ethu edrama esiXhosa athi abhalwe ngayo .
Kuye kwabonakalo ukuba umxholo wala mabali uyafana awuyelelenanga .
Umphandi ubonile ukuba ababhali bathetha into enye , kwaye bethetha into enye nje , umphandi akangqinelani nabo .
Oku kungangqinelani kuye kwazalwa kukutshintsha kwamaxesha .
Ezi zinto aba babhali bezi ncwadi zedrama ababhala ngazo zizinto ezazisenzeka kude kudala .
Ngenxa yokutshintsha kwamaxesha , akukho mntu ulindeleleke ukuba aphile ngale ndlela ezi ncwadi zisikhokelela ngayo .
Incwadi nganye ephononongiweyo ibijongwa phantsi kweenkalo ezithile , ezithe zangqinelana nolu phando , ukuze umphandi afike apho ebesiya nolu phando .
Apha kolu phando umphandi ude wafika apho kufel'ithole khona nolu phando , yonke imibuzo ebaqale enayo yaphanduleka ekuhambeni kophando .
Sibabonile ababhali beencwadi zedrama bezibhala iincwadi zabo , kunye nendlela leyo bathi bazibhala ngayo .
Siwubonile umohluko phakathi kwababhali besini sobuduna kunye nababhali ababhinqileyo nendlela ababazoba ngayo abalinganiswa ababhinqileyo .
Ababhali besini sobuduna bababzoba abalinganiswa abangamabhinqa njengabantu ekumele bexhomekeke kwabo besini soduna , hayi abantu abazimeleyo , abaziphandelayo .
Umfundi umbonile umbali webali leqonga xa ezoba abalinganiswa uFuneka kunye noZanele phaya kula ncwadi u - Ndiyekeni njengabantu abaxhwitha amadoda ade ome nko , bawashiye engenanto , bakugqiba bawalahlele ngaphandle .
Khumbula indlela yena umbhali ka - ' Inene nasi Isibhozo , ' esizobela umlinganiswa
uMasukude njengomfazi okhohlakeleyo , ongcolileyo , othakathayo , kwaye oligqwirha .
Sithe sisakhuza oko kubunjwa kuMasukude , saze sadibana nomlinganiswa uNojenti , phaya ku - ' Ndixoleleni , ' ekhohlakele yena kuqala efana nje noMasukude , naye engumbulali othakathayo .
Umphandi usebenzise yanye jwi incwadi ebhalwe libhinqa , oku akwenzekanga ngampazamo , kwenziwe ukubonisa ukunqongaphala kweencwadi zedrama ezibhalwa ngmabhinqa , abe ezama ukunyusa isidima samabhinqa , esiwiswe ngezi ncwadi zininzi zibhalwa ngababhali besini sobuduna .
Le meko ikwayiyo ekhuthaze umphandi ukuba enze uphando olunje ngolu , ukuze amehlo abo babhalayo avuleke babone ukuba ingxaki ikho , kwaye ifuna bona ukuba bancede kwangoku ithuba lisekhona .
Kumabali edrama amane athe axoxwa apha kolu phando u - ' Inene nasi Isibhozo , ' ' Ndiyekeni , ' ' Ndixoleleni ' kunye no - ' Iinkunzi Ezimbini , ' siwabonile ke amabhinqa ecinezelwa kwaye ephathwa kakubi ngabantu besini sobuduna .
Uqaphele ukuba amabhinqa awaphili phantsi kwengcinezelo kusini na ngoba ngelinye ixesha umntu lo uphila phantsi kwengcinezelo , akayiqondi naloo nto , de yolathwe ngomnye umntu .
Iba ngulo mncedi ke nawe .
Ukuba wena apha ebomini bakho uyaqonda ukuba uyacinezelwa ngumntu othandana naye , ophangela naye okanye ofunda naye , zama ukuba uphume kolo manyano , nokuba ulibhinqa okanaye uyindoda .
Kaloku namabhinqa anaso isakhona sokucinezela amadoda , ingakumbi emitshatweni .
Umfazi ayiphathe indoda yakhe caba indoda ayinakukwazi ukwenza nto ngaphandle kokuba icele imvume emfazini , njengokuba sibonile phaya kwibali lethu u - ' Iinkunzi Ezimbini ' isenziwa nguSibonda loo nto emfazini wakhe uNolasti .
Yinto apha le eyimoshayo imitshato , nayo nayiphi na indibano phakathi kwabantu ababini , ngoba kaloku omnye umntu ngoku uza koyika ukuphila ubomi bakhe , kufuneka aphilele omnye umntu ngenxa yoloyika analo .
Umphandi angacebisa ukuba abo bathi bawafunde amabali anje , bawafunde ngamehlo kunye neendlebe ezibukhali ngoba bangakhawuleza babhidakala kwinto amabayithathe okanye bayizuze xa begqibile ukuzifunda ezi zifundo zedrama .
Umphandi uphinde acebise ababhali abasafundayo ukuba basuke baphele kumba wokuzoba amabhinqa njengabantu ababuthathaka abaxhomekeke kuphela kumadoda , ngoba amaxesha atshintshile ngoku , azisekho njalo izinto .
Ukuba kukho ingcamango abafuna ukuyizoba , mabayizobe ngokupheleleyo , bayibeke phambili ingxaki , bakugqiba baze nesisombululo .
Umzekelo , ukuba umbhali utshiswa yinto afuna ukuyibhala ngamabhinqa emhluphayo , efana nokungazihloniphi kwamabhinqa , uvumelekile ukuba akubhale oko , kodwa makangapheleli apho .
Makagqithele aze neengcebiso apho amabhinqa angathi aziphucule ngayo , ukuze ibhinqa elisakhulayo elifunda loo ncwadi libe nenkuthazo nokuba belisalahleka ebomini balo .
Ingcebiso yomphandi yokugqibela yeyokuba ababhali besini sobuduna bakhe babhale iidrama ezinyusa isikhundla samabhinqa , ngoba kuninzi okwenziwa ngamabhinqa , kodwa okungabhalwayo ezincwadini .
Singabantu abaphangela kweli bakala lezezibhalo sinokukhuthazana , sinyusane ukuze wonke umntu aphumelele , hayi into yokuba abanye banyuke ngokucinezela abanye .
Umphandi uthanda ukukhuthaza abo basakhulayo , bathe banomdla ekubhaleni ukuba bayibone le ntlekela yenzeka kwizibhalo zethu zolwimi lwesiXhosa , ze bakhuthazeke ukuba nabo babhale iincwadi ezifana nezi , nto nje bona bazame ukunyusa isidima samabhinqa , baphelise le nto yokucinezela esinye esini maxa benyusa esinye .
USibonda naye unale ngxaki inye , naye uphakamile wathetha , engqinelana nesi sithethi , ngokuba yena ukhala ngento yokuba , umfazi wakhe
uNolasti akanayo intlonipho kwaye uziphethe emtshatweni wabo ngenxa yale mfundo anayo .
Imfundo emfazini ibonwa njengokuba yingxaki ngokuba umfazi ofundileyo unento yokufuna ukwenza izigqibo zekhaya .
Iqalele apho ingxabano phakathi kukaSibonda kunye nomfazi wakhe omcinci uNolasti .
Abanye abafazi bakaSibonda , uNifinishi kunye noNokhaya bona bathobekile .
Kaloku bona ngabafazi abadala kwaye abanayo kwaphela imfundo .
Ukutshata komfazi wesithathu kukaSibonda yabangela utshintsho emzini wabo ngokuba uNolasti akafani nabo tu .
Izinto zekhaya ezifana nokucoca , ukupheka okanye ukwenza iti , uNolasti uziyekela kubo , ngelithi yena uyaphangela , kwaye uyabondla ngemali ayibhatalwayo ekhitshini , ngoko ke bona mabenze imisebenzi yaphakathi kwekhaya .
Oku kubangela ukuba abafazi bakaSibonda bangamthandi lo Nolasti .
Le ngxwabangxwaba yile yabangela ukuba uNolasti awushiye umzi wakhe , agoduke ngokuba yena akazibona ephila ndlelanye naba bafazi bakaSibonda ngoba yena uphucukile kwaye ufundile , ngoko ufuna ukuphathwa njengomntu okwelo nqanaba hayi nje ngathi akabalulekanga .
Mve kule ngxoxo ingezantsi : Nolimithi : Ndinqanda ndinganqandi ubonanje .
Iyakhubekisa okunene into yokuba abafazi benziwe amakhoboka amadoda olu hlobo , ukuze kube kukho izinto ezifana nooNofinishi aba , kuba enjenje nje umyeni wakho woniwa ngabo .
Ukuba bebengengabo abathoba - sikutyele bangabo ngengenje uSibonda .
Ibe ke iculo alihlabelayo livunywa yiyo yonke le lali , akakhathaliseki nokuba uyiloza kangakanani na .
Nawethu amadoda kufuneka asiphathe njengokuba esitsho .
Inene yinto ngobunto bayo le yobubonda , ndakuyicel'ivuthiwe ndifung'amaKhwemnte .
Nolasti : Masingazikhathazi kakhulu wethu Mfazi .
Kaloku yonke into ilunga ngokulungiswa .
Mna ndicinga ukuba xa sinokubashumayeza abanye abafazi aba , sibabonise ingxaki esikuyo thina bafazi , bangasebenzisana nathi ekuthuleni le dyokhwe siyithwaliswe ngumendo .
Isengenzeka ubonanje into yokuba baninzi abacinga njengathi qha bayoyika ukuzidandalazisa izimvo zabo kuba bacinga ukuba mhlawumbi kuza kuthiwa baphokele .
Kuyaqapheleka ke ukuba umlinginiswa oyintloko apha kule ncwadi yedrama nguNolasti .
Lo mlinganiswa zininzi izinto ezimvelelayo , ezithi zibe yingxaki ebomini bakhe ngenxa yokuba elibhinqa .
Apha ngentla sibona ethetha nesihlobo sakhe esikhuthaza ukuba sinyamezele emzini waso nokuba sekunzima kangakanani na ngoba uyayazi into yokuba emendweni kuyanyanyezelwa .
Le ntetho iphakathi kukaNolasti kunye noNolimithi , uNolimithi ekhalaza ngempatho mbi abayifumana ebayenini babo , beziva behleli phantsi kwengcinezelo emizini yabo .
Oku kuthethwa ngaba bafazi ngoku kanye kuza kuthethwa ngako apha kwesi sahluko .
Apha kweli bali ingcingane yesini sobukhomokazi igqame kakhulu ukogqitha le ifumaneka pha kwela bali u - ' Inene nasi Isibhoza . '
Xa sijonge umlinganiswa oyintloko uNolasti , siyambona lo mlinganiswa ukuba uyangena phantsi kwebhinqa elithi lilwele inkululeko namalungelo amabhinqa .
Sikubona oku ngokwezenzo zakhe , kuqala , udaba lokuba kanti ufundile luyakuxhasa oku , udaba lwesibini lelokuba , lo mfazi uyakwazi ukuzimela endodeni yakhe , akenzi nantoni na ayixelelwayo okungathi ulusana .
Umyeni kaNolasti onguSibonda , yindoda apha esinokuthi yindoda eqotho yomXhosa , othi apha alihloniphe kakhulu isiko lakhe .
Ngoko ke unendlela azilindele ukuba abafazi bakhe baziphathe ngayo , kwaye kunezinto alindelele ukuba bazenze njengoko bengamakhosikazi akhe .
Funda incoko phakathi kukaNolasti nendoda yakhe uSibonda xa bebuya emngcwabeni :
Sibonda : Kanene akukho nto niyenzayo ngaphandle kokuthetha nina bafazi .
Iphi ikofu Nolasti ?
Ndidiniwe ndingumfi ndilapha nje .
Nolasti : Ndidinwe oku kwam ubonanje .
Ubungenakuyenza ngokwakho namhlanje ikofu ?
Sibonda : Uthi mna mandenze ikofu ?
Uyaziva kakuhle le nto uyithethayo ?
Le ncoko ingentla phakathi kwesi sibini sitshatileyo isibonisa indlela isini sesiduna esisibona ngayo isini sobukhomokazi .
Apha sibona ngokucacileyo ukuba le ndonda inala ngcamango yokuba umsebenzi womfazi kukukhathelela indoda yakhe maxesha onke .
Kaloku qwalasela ukuba bobabini badiniwe bavela esingcwabeni , umfazi yena uvela ukuya kupheka nokuhlamba izitya emngcwabeni , kucacile ukuba soze ithi kanti akadinwanga , kodwa kuyo yonke loo nto kunyanzelekile ukuba afike emzini wakhe aphinde enze imisebenzi yakhe yobufazi .
Aba bafazi apha kweli bali bayayibona le mpatho , abanye bayayikhaba , babe abanye beyivuma ngoba abazi ngcono , nabo banala ngcamango yento yokuba umsebenzi wabo njengabafazi kukunakekela indoda yabo , ukucoca indlu , ukupheka nokukhulisa abantwana .
Le yantlukwano ikho phakathi kwaba bafundileyo kunye nabo bangakhange bawabona amasango esikolo .
Nantsi incoko phakathi kukaNolasti kunye nomhlobo wakhe uNolimithi ekubeni uNolasti embalisela ngendlela umyeni wakhe uSibonda athi wamkweka ngayo emngcwabeni , xeshikweni esithi amadoda abhubha esemancinci ngenxa yabafazi babo abaphucikileyo kwaye abangenandlela yokuyiphatha indoda , bona bantu noko baqiqileyo ,
kwaye bafundileyo , kwaye bayiqwalaselayo le mpatho mbi :
Nolimithi : Ndinqanda ndinganqandi ubonanje .
Iyakhubekisa okunene into yokuba abafazi benziwe amakhoboka amadoda olu hlobo , ukuze kube kukho izinto ezifana nooNofinishi aba , kuba enjenje umnyeni wakho woniwa ngabo .
Ukuba bebengabo aba thobasikutyele bangabo ngengenje uSibonda . . .
Nolasti : Masingazikhathazi kakhulu wethu Mfazi .
Kaloku yonke into ilunga ngokulungiswa .
Mna ndicinga ukuba xa sinokubashumayeza abanye abafazi aba , sibabonise ingxaki esikuyo thina bafazi , bangasebenzisana nathi ekothuleni le dyokhwe siyithweliswe ngumendo .
Ukuba uyakhumbula xa bekuchazwa ukuba yintoni ingcingane yesini sobukhomokazi , bekuxhentsiwe phezu kwento yokuba , le ngcingane ithetha ngamabhinqa athi adibana alwela inkululeko yabo kunye namanye amabhinqa .
Le nto kanye yenziwa nguNolasti kunye nesihlobo sakhe uNolimithi .
Jonga pha kwezi ndawu bathi " Iyakhubekisa okunene into yokuba abafazi benziwe amakhoboka amadoda olu hlobo " baze baphinde bathi
" Mna ndicinga ukuba xa sinokubashumayeza abanye abafazi aba . "
Aba bafazi babini yimizekelo emihle yamabhinqa afuna ukuncedisana namanye amabhinqa ukuze bakhululeke phantsi kwengcinezelo yamadoda .
Abayenzi lento ukukhulula iziqu zabo kuphela , bafuna ukunceda nabanye bababone ukuba le mpatho baphantsi kwayo , ayiyiyo .
Akulula ke ukubonisa wonke umntu ukuba bahleli phantsi kwengcinezelo xa bona bengayiboni loo nto .
UNolasti uthe xa ezama ukubabonisa abanye abafazi aba atshate nabo apha kuSibonda into yokuba le ndlela uSibonda abaphatha ngayo asiyondlela yokuphatha abafazi .
Uthe akuzimela lo mfazi , abanye abafazi aba babini bambona njengomntu oziphakamisileyo kwaye ophucukileyo .
Bave bezithethela uNofinishi kwakunye nomfazi wesibini uNokhaya :
Nokhaya : Ndixakiwe nam Nofinishi , kudala ndiyijika - jika ingqondo yam kodwa andiphumi nasiphumo .
Kucace gca okwekat'emhlophe ehlungwini khona ukuba asisobe sonwabe sonke kweliya khaya lethu belifudula liseluxolweni ngenxa yokusa nokuswela imbeko kukaNolasti .
Nofinishi : Usimele ngempucuko yokuba yena akanakuphathwa yincentsa .
Ndixakwa kukuba wayeze kuthini apha kanti ufuna ukuziphatha .
Inzima le mfundo yabo , ibaphambanisa ingqondo .
Bayafuna ukuba ngabafazi kodwa abakwazi tu ukwenda !
Lo Nolasti ungafika engqayiza , ezibiza ukuba yena uyinkosikazi kaJwarha uqobo , ezingomba isifuba kuba etshate ezi - ofisini zeemantyi , inqaba kukuziphatha okwenkosikazi .
Kucacile ukuba aba bafazi babini abavani kwaphela noNolasti kwaye le nto yakhe yokuba abe kanti ufundile nabo bayibona nje ngokuba yingxaki ngoba bathi yiyo le imenza ukuba acinge uphucukile kunabo .
Bayalibala into yokuba ukutya oku bakutyayo , nempahla le bayinxibisa abantwana babo ithethwa nguNolasti , ngenxa yale mfundo yakhe bangayiboneli ntweni .
Indaweni yokuba banyamane bebo bathathu , bencedisane kwaye bakhuthazane ukuze kuhlaleke kamnandi emzini wabo , wayalwana , kwaye abahloniphani , nto le iliwa yile ngcingane yesini sobukhomokazi .
Ngoba ngoku - bhekisele kule ngcingane , amabhinqa kumele ukuba amanyane ancedisane ukulwa ingcinezelo yamadoda .
Bona aba bafazi bayayikhuthaza .
Kweli bali likaMothlabane umbhali usizobele umlinganiswa oyintloko ukuba abe ngumntu obhinqileyo , kwaye ofunde ngaphezu kwendoda yakhe , ngoko ke ukungalingani ngokwesini sekubonakele ngokupheleleyo .
Indaba yokufunda kukaNolasti nokuphangela kwakhe yingxaki kakhulu apha kweli bali , ingakumbi emnyenini wakhe uSibonda .
Kaloku le meko ibhalwe phantsi kwayo le ncwadi , yokuba nomfazi ofundileyo yinto apha engaqhelekanga kula maxesha ngoba imfundo asiyonto apha ibonwa ibalulekile ngoba , indoda yiyo ekumele ukuba iphangele ibuye nemali endlini , xeshikweni umfazi esenza imisebenzi yasendlini , ngoba kaloku indoda yiyo intloko yekhaya .
UMfazi kaSibonda omncinci ufundile kwaye uphangela emakhitshini , ngokoke naye ungena nemali endlini ethi isetyenziswe ukuthenga ukutya , impahla yabantwana njalo njalo .
Oku kubangela ukuba uSibonda azive eyindoda engaphelelenga ngoba abafazi bakhe abadala bondliwa ngumfazi wakhe omncinci .
Yena uNolasti uyibona le nto nje - ngokuba uncedisana nomnyeni wakhe kwizinto zasekhaya .
Oku kwenzeka phakathi kwesi sisbini kuko okubangela kuthiwa ukuba kukho ukungalingani ngokwesini .
UNolasti wenza ngandlela zonke ukuqinisekisa ukuba uncedisana nomnyeni wakhe apha endlini , kodwa yena uSibonda lo uqinisekile ekubeni yena
akasoze aphathwe ngumfazi kwaye angahlonitshwa ngenxa yokuba lo mfazi ephangela .
Funda into ethethwa nguSibonda xa uNolasti ethe wavuma ukugcina abantwana baka - Nkosikazi White , umqeshi wakhe , ebusuku xeshikweni bona besaphumile , abe phofu uNolasti engacelanga mvume kumnyeni wakhe :
Nolasti : Kaloku baza kuya entlanganisweni nomnyeni wakhe , babuye ebusuku kakhulu .
Mna ndiza kugcina abantwana lo gama bona besentlanganisweni . . .
Sibonda : Ingaba iindlebe zam zinomphula okanye ndicothelwa bubuthulu ?
Uyandixelela yonke le nto okanye ufuna uluvo ngokugcina abantwana babeLungu ebusuku ?
Nolasti : Hayi wethu ndiyacela ungabi sathetha enye into .
Sendivumile kuMedem .
Sibonda : Uvume njani Nolasti ?
Uyivuma njani into elelo hlobo ungakhange ugqithe kum ?
Uthetha ukuba uza kusuka uzigqibele ukuba unokubuya nanini na xa uthanda apha emzini wam
Kucacile into yokuba uSibonda yindoda apha ethanda ukuphatha .
Ufuna ukuba izinto zihambe ngendlela yakhe .
Nengcingane yokungalingani ngesini isixelela loo nto ke ukuba isini sesiduna sizibona sibaluleke ngaphezu kweso sobukhomakazi , yiyo loo nto uSibonda elindele uNolasti ukuba acele imvume kuye kuqala phambi kokuba enze izigqibo , okungathi uNolasti ngumntwana ongayaziyo into ayenzayo .
Amaxesha esiphila kuwo ngoku awasafani namaxesha ootatomkhulu noomakhulu bethu ababephila kuwo .
Nto leyo ethetha into yokuba amasiko nezithethe zethu zakwaXhosa zitshintsha nokutshintsha kwamaxesha .
Kakade ayikho into ehleli ihleli , zonke izinto ziyatshintsha .
Xa sijongane nendawo amabhinqa akuyo ngoku size sithelekise nendawo awayekuyo ngoko , utshintsho luyabonakala .
Kuninzi okwakulindeleke kumabhinqa kwixesha lakudala , ingakumbi emitshatweni .
Amabhinqa ayelindeleke ukuba kanti atshatile phambi kokuba afike kwiminyaka ethile , ukuba kanti kufika loo minyaka bengatshatanga , babejongwa njengabantu abangaphelelanga .
Bona ke abo batshatileyo banezabo izinto ekulindeleke bezenzile .
Zonke ke ezi zinto bese zikhankanyiwe kumancandelo angaphambili , xa bekuthenthwa ngeendidi zamabhinqa alwela ukungalingani ngokwesini .
Apha kweli candelo umphandi ufuna ukuchopha kumba wezikhundla ezibakho emtshatweni .
Xa abantu betshata , sube kutshatha ibhinqa kunye nomntu wesilisa .
Ekubeni oko kwenzekile , utata wekhaya uye abonwe njengentloko yekhaya , apho kulindeleke ukuba ondle umfazi wakhe , akhusele umzi wabo .
Ukanti lona ibhinqa lilindeleke ukuba linakekele umnyeni walo ngokuqinisekisa ukuba ukutya kuhleli kukho etafileni , indlu icocekile kwaye konke akufunayo kukhona endlini , ze amzalele abantwana lande usapho .
Kodwa konke oko kwatshintsha nokutshintsha kwamaxesha .
Kula maxesha kukho amabhinqa aphangela mihla yonke , de baphangele ezinzulwini zasebusuku , nto leyo ethetha ukuba , ixesha lokuba apheke , acoce indlu , anakekele umyeni wakhe liyancipha , kunyanzelekile ukuba umnyeni anyuse iikawusi , angene esikhundleni sobufazi .
Nto le ibingasoze ingcamleke kumaxesha akudala .
Masikhe siqaphele apha kweli bali likaMothlane , apho umlinganiswa uNolasti athi athathe umsebenzi wasebusuku kuba acingela imali azakuyizuza kulo msebenzi , ezakuthi incedisane nabo emzini wakhe nomnyeni wakhe uSibonda , masikhe siphonononge le ncoko yabo :
Nolasti : Nisebenze njani namhlanje Jwarha ?
Sibonda : Sizamile Nkosikazi , ibe njani eyakho imini ?
Nolasti : Hayi kube kuhle kakhulu nakum .
Loo nto ke ndifumene nesithembiso sokubhaselwa ngeR20 yonke ngomso .
Hayi sendibona ukuba ndiza kusebenzisa kakuhle neMedem wam .
Sibonda : iR20 yonke ?
Yeyantoni ?
Nolasti : Kaloku baza kuya entlanganisweni nomyeni wakhe , babuye ebusuku kakhulu .
Mna ke ndiza kugcina abantwana lo gama bona basentlanganisweni .
Emva kwentlanganiso baza kukhe badanise nje kancinci bazikhumbuze iimini zobutsha babo .
Sibonda : Ingaba iindlebe zam zinomphula okanye ndicothelwa bubuthulu bethu ?
Uyandixelela yonke le nto okanye ufuna uluvo lwam ngokugcina abantwana babeLungu ebusuku ?
Nolasti : Hayi wethu ndiyacela ungabi sathetha enye into .
Sendivumile kuMedem .
Sibonda : Uvume njani Nolasti ?
Uyivuma njani into elolo hlobo ungakhange ugqithe kum ?
Uthetha ukuba uza kusuka uzigqibele ukuba unokubuya nanini na xa uthanda apha emzini wam ?
Nolasti : Andikhange ndicinge njalo , eyona nto isuke yaphambili kum leli themba lale mali ingaka ndiza kuyifumana ekubeni ndisazi ukuba
sixakeke sinje kweli khaya .
Ndiqonde ukuba xa sinokuyifumana le R20 ungatsho ukwazi ukurhafela laa ntsimi isemmangweni , sibe nakho nokuthengela abantwana iimpahla zobusika .
Sibonda : Ngubani obethe andikwazi kuzenza ezo zinto ngokwam ?
Sekutheni sendicingelwa nguwe njengoku indlela yokwenza izinto emzini wam ?
Nolasti : Besekukade .
He wethu Sigqibo !
Yintoni le nto uthi uzazi ukuba utsala nzima ube uzenza ngathi unekratshi ?
Uyazi ukuba kule mbalela asisavuni nto iyiyo , siyalamba .
Ukuba ibingeyiyo le mali ndiza nayo kwaba beLungu ngesekukudala abantwana bethu bengasahlawuli esikolweni .
Ngesingesakwazi nokumondla uMama wakho , andisathethi ngemali yoogqirha bakhe .
Kutheni le nto usuka undenze umoni ngokuza nemali yokukuncedisa ekwenzeni ukuba intlalo yekhaya ibe lula ?
Sibonda : Unayo le nto yokuthi ndibeka isheleni ubeke indaliso .
Yiyeke usayithanda kunjalonje loo nto ukuba akufuni kuvana negwangqa !
Nolasti : Yeyiphi ecaphukisayo ke ngoku ?
Andithi ndithetha inyani xa ndi . . .
Sibonda : ( Egragrama ) ndithe kuwe sukuthetha ndithetha .
Bathi cwaka ke bade bafika ekhaya .
Aye endlwini alala kuyo uNolasti , ajikeleze phandle uSibonda ehlola izinto - yinto , emana ukuzithethela .
Ewe utheth'inyaniso lo mfazi .
Kodwa ke loo nyaniso ithi makandiphathe emzini wam , le mali yakhe imnika igunya lokwenza unothanda ?
Angaske ayeke noko kuphangela kuba andizange ndaxhomekeka mfazini kakade .
Ukuphangela kwakhe akufanele kumnika gunya lakubuya ngonothanda akugqiba ukuba ngumendi .
Loo nto ingabonakalisa nabanye aba .
Yena ke ade asukele phezulu njekungokuba loo Mlungu wakhe yena akayazi into yokuba kufuneka acele emzini wakhe ?
Ingathi iza kuzal'amathokazana le nto yaba beLungu ndifung ' udadethu !
Aphazanyiswe kuloo ntlanganiso yakhe kukubizelwa isidlo sangokuhlwa .
Apha ngentla siyakubona oku kungquzulana phakathi kwesi sibini uNolasti kunye noSibonda , xa sibona uNolasti exelela umyeni wakhe into yokuba uceliwe nguMedem wakhe ukuba asebenze ebusuku , agade abantwana xa bona nomyeni wakhe besephumile .
Apha umbhali usibonisa imeko apho lowo uyintloko yekhaya ilibhinqa hayi indoda , ngoba umyeni akaphangeli ngumfazi ophangelayo .
Ingcambu yale ngxabona siyibona apha ngentla izalwa yile nto .
uNolasti nguye ophangelayo , nguye oza nemali kweli khaya , nguye oncedana nomama womyeni wakhe ukubhatala amaxabiso kagqirha xa engaphilanga , ikwanguye ondla umyeni wakhe kunye nabafazi bakhe ababini .
USibonda akayithandi nakancinci le nto .
Akafuni ukuba umfazi wakhe aphangele ebusuku , kodwa le mali aza kube eyiphangelela yile iza kuphinda incedisane nabo apha endlini .
Ude unendawo ezifuna ukucebisa umfazi wakhe ukuba awuyeke lo msebenzi , kuba lo mfazi akakhange aqale kuye kuqala phambi kokuba avume ukuwuthatha lo msebenzi , kodwa lo mfazi , ukuvuma kwakhe ukuthatha lo msebenzi uwuthathe enenjongo yokunceda , hayi ukudala ingxabano phakathi kwakhe nomyeni wakhe .
USibonda uthi xa sele esukile kuNolasti , avume ukuba lo mfazi unyanisile ukuba le mali iza kunceda apha phakathi kwekhaya , kodwa into enzima kukukuvuma oku apha emfazini wakhe .
Eyona nto iqaphelekayo apha kule ncoko yabo , yinto yokuba , uSibonda uzibona ingathi isikhundla sakhe sobudoda siyadodobala ngenxa yala mandla alo mfazi okuzimele apha kweli khaya .
Akayithandi indaba yokuba uNolasti engaaxhomekekanga kuye , kanti iguqukile , nguSibonda oxhomekeke kuNolasti .
Kodwa yena uNolasti akayiboni njalo , uyibona ngendlela yokuba uncedisana nomyeni wakhe , ngoba ude athi ,
" Ndiqonde ukuba xa sinokuyifumana le R20 ungatsho ukwazi ukurhafela laa ntsimi isemmangweni , sibe nakho nokuthengela abantwana iimpahla zobusika , " ukubonisa ukuba yena ebezama ukunceda , hayi ukumosha .
Kweli xesha siphila kulo , amabhinqa angaphangela naphina apho afuna ukuphangela khona , ayisekho laa nto ithi , le yimisebenzi yobudoda , le yeyobubhinqa , imisebenzi ivulekile kuluNtu lonke .
Oku ke kuthetha ukuba uyakwazi ukufika kusapho oluthile apho ibhinqa lisamkela imali engaphaya kunaleyo yomyeni wakhe , okanye ibe kanti lo myeni akaphangeli kwa ukuphangeli .
Loo nto ithethe ukuba , eli bhinqa lilo elibeka isonka etafileni .
Ingxaki ke iqale apho , ngoba ngoku lo myeni akasenalo ilungelo lokungxola ngokuba yintloko yekhaya , ngoba konke okulindeleke ukuba ekwenzile
njengentloko yekhaya akasakwazi ukwenza .
Yiyo loo nto uza kubona imitshato emininzi ingasebenzi , ngoba abantu besilisa abafuni kuyamkela yonke le nguqu , ade athi omnye ,
" Andisoze nditshate umntu owamkela ngaphezulu kunam , ndim indoda kufuneka kucace . "
Kanti ke akunyanzelekanga ukuba kube njalo , kuba kaloku wonke umntu kufuneka atshintshe nokutshintsha kwamaxesha .
Ithuba lokuba amabhinqa abonelwe entweni nabo lifikile .
Ixesha lokuba amabhinqa athathelwe ingqalelo kwigalelo abanalo eluntwini sele lifikile .
Bantu bakuthi amaxesha esiphila kuwo namhla awafani nalawo amandulo , kwaye awasoze aphinde abuyele .
Siyayibona le nto isenzeka apha kule ncwadi kaMothlabane pha kula mzi kaSibonda .
uNolasti nguye ophangelayo , uSibonda akayithandi kuyaphi le nto yokuphangela komfazi wakhe , ngoba uyabona ukuba umfazi wakhe akaxhomekekanga kuye nganto , into ekunayo ngulo mfazi obeka ukutya etafileni , esondla uSibonda nabafazi bakhe ababini .
Le nto imhlalisa kakubi uNolasti , de uSibonda ambethe , avalelwe ngamapolisa , ze amgxothe uNolasti emzini wakhe ngenxa yoko .
Omnye umntu angacinga ukuba uSibonda uza kuvuya axhentse enomfazi ophangelayo , obeka ukutya etafileni , encedisana naye apha phakathi kwekhaya .
Kodwa hayi , yena ubona indima yakhe phakathi kwekhaya ithathwa ngumfazi wakhe .
Esi sahluko sahluke mpela kwisahluko esiphambi kwaso ngoba esi siphambi kwaso besijongenene nendlela ababhali besini sobuduna ababazoba ngayo abalinganiswa ababhinqile , sabe esi sona sijonga indlela umbhali olibhinqa athi abazobe ngayo abalinganiswa abangamabhinqa .
Umohluko ke ukho kwaye mkhulu .
Simbonile umbhali wale ncwadi yedrama isetyenziswe apha , emzoba umlinganiswa wakhe oyintloko obhinqileyo njengomfazi owomeleleyo , ozimeleyo kwaye okwaziyo ukuzenzela izigqibo zakhe .
Nangona umyeni wakhe lo mfazi ebesilwa naye lonke ithuba alifumanayo , oku akukhange kume endleleni yeli bhinqa , uqhubekekile ephangela , esondla usapho lwakhe , wathi xa egxothwa emzini wakhe ngumyeni wakhe ngenxa yokungquzulana , wakuhlonela oko wahamba , xa usapho lwakhe nelomyeni wakhe lithe laxoxa , kwagqitywa
ekubeni abuyele emzini wakhe , nalapho ubahlonele wenjenjalo .
Nto ebonisa ukuba eli bhinqa alizange lizibone lilikhulu libaluleke ngaphezulu komyeni walo ngenxa yena ephangela , umyeni wakhe engaphangeli .
Uye wahlala engumntu onentlonipho nembeko maxa onke .
Oku kungqinwa yile ncoko ingezantsi :
Sigqibo : O - o !
Uqonde ukuba mawubuye wena eli xa mna bendithe andikufuni ?
Nolasti : Ngenditheni xa amawenu ebeye kundilanda ?
Sigqibo : Waqala nini wena ukumamela into ethethwa ngamawethu ?
Uze kuba usazimisele ukwenza into ethandwa nguwe ?
Nolasti : Uyandityhola kanti .
Besendiyincamile into yokubuyela apha mna , qha amaJwarha namaCirha aye avana ukuba mandibuye . . .
Oku kungentla kungqina into yokuba uNolasti lo akazange naninina abe nentloko enkulu ngenxa yesikhundla akuso emtshatweni wakhe , nangona inguye yedwa ophangelayo kubafazi bakaSibonda .
Nabo ke abahlobo bakaFuneka befaka uLoni isifuthufuthu ngokuthi bangamyeki ngetyala ade asele , wade naye wayekelela wasela .
Koloku uFuneka usabambe esaa sicela sikaNdila sokuba makasebenze uLoni , ade abe sisicaka sotywala .
Apha kule drama umbhali usizobele abalinganiswa abhinqileyo phambili njengabantu abasebenzisa amadoda ukufumana izinto abazifunayo , bengakhathalisi nokuba la madoda bawasebenzisayo atshatile kwaye aneentsapho ahlala nawo .
Lo mbhali usizobela abalinganiswa uZanele kunye noFuneka njengamabhinqa enza amadoda amaxhoba emalini .
Ubazobe njengabantu abaxhomekeke kubantu abangamadoda ukuze babe nemali kwaye babe nazo zonke izinto abazifunayo .
Lo mbhali wale drama akaphelelenga ekusizobeleni aba balinganiswa babhinqileyo njengee " GoldDiggers " njengokuba kusitshiwo esiNgesini , kodwa usibonisa nempembelelo ehamba noko .
Apha usikrobisa indlela la mabhinqa asetyenziswa ngumntu wesilisa ukubuyisa ikratshi kumntu angavani naye .
Oku kubonisa kwa indlela abantu besilisa abawasebenzisa ngayo amabhinqa ngendlela ezimdaka , ngoba oku kuhlisa isidima sobubhinqa , kodwa bona abayiboni loo nto ngenxa yokuthanda ukunakekelwa .
Nanku umzekelo ophilayo apha kweli bali le drama , apho umlinganiswa wesilisa uNdila ephembelela eli bhinqa uFuneka ukuba lizenzele kwixhoba elinguLoni , ngenxa yengxabano abakuyo :
Funeka : Ukuba ufuna imali utsho ebhatyini mtshana .
Funeka : Hayi wethu ndiyaqhula .
Ndila : Uyaqal'ukuthetha .
Uyayazi into yokuba ndiphelelwe emsebenzini kwaye ndicinga ukuba uyazazi nezizathu .
Ndila : Uthando malube nemisebenzi , le mpahla ikule ndlu iyathetha .
Ubumnandi balo mcimbi yinto yokuba into yokuthandana kwethu lihlebo lethu ( watsho emwola ) Look , Funie girl , umdlalo uwuqhelile sondeza uMawonga , izabatha zaziwa nguwe .
Funeka : Ndakuyibambisa intaka leyo , ndiyithini ?
Ndila : Yixhwithe iintsiba , kuba buyaphela ubuntaka bayo zakuvuthuluka iintsiba .
Funeka : Ndiyakukhe ndizame mtshana , kodwa makhe lulane uthuli .
Ndila : Mtshana wam !
( Bawolane kwakhona . )
Kwesi sicatshulwa singentla umphandi uyibonisa gca into yokuba uNdila ukhokela uFuneka ukuba enze ububi bokuxhwitha uLoni ngenxa yekratshi alibamba kuLoni .
Naye ke uFuneka uyavuma engaphozisanga maseko ngenxa yalo mntu anguye , uhlelinje efuna ukuphila ubomi obungaphezulu kunaye .
Lo mbhali uthe wakhetha indlela afuna ukubazoba ngayo abalinganiswa ababhinqileyo kwincwadi yakhe yedrama , wathi njengoninzi lwababhali
bedrama abangabantu besilisa , wabazoba njengabantu abangasweli nto abayifunayo , abangenamqolo wokuzimela ngaphandle koncedo lwendoda ebomini babo .
Ixhaphakile ke le nto kwiincwadi zedrama ezibhalwe ngababhali besini sobulisa , nto le ijongwa lolu phando .
Lo mbhali uyichane kanye kanye le ntetho ayikhankanye apha ngentla , ngoba le nto ayithethayo ngendlela ababhali besini sobuduna abathi babazobe abalinganiswa ababhinqileyo njengabantu abonobuqhophololo , yile kanye yenziwe ngumbhali wale drama xa wayezoba umlinganiswa uFuneka kunye noZanele .
Abantu abakhe bayifunda le ncwadana yedrama baya kubona ukuba uJongilanga ubazobe aba balinganiswa bangamabhinqa njengabantu abaqhatha amadoda , de indoda ifikelele kwingcinga zokuba iyathandwa ngala mabhinqa , ize ilandelise ngokuwenzela nantoni na ayifunayo , kungakhathalekisanga nokuba le ndoda itshatile kusini na .
UZilandu nenkosikazi yakhe basweleka beshiya unyana wabo okuphela kwakhe , uThembile .
uThembile ukhuliswa nguyisekazi , uZamile onomfazi onguNojenti .
UZamile noNojenti abanabantwana .
Ekukhuleni kwakhe uThembile uthatha inkosikazi egama linguNomava .
Iqala apho imfazwe nodushe .
UZamile akavumi neenkomo zikaZilandu ukuba uThembile azeke ngazo .
UThembile akanangxaki malunga nekhazi .
Mve uThembile ethatha noTat'omncinci wakhe ngokuthatha umfazi , bave bethetha :
Thembile : Bawokazi , njengoko ndisekhefini emsebenzini wam , ndicinga ukuba ndithi ndiphethukele emsebenzini ndibe ndinento endiyiqabelisayo kwezobudoda .
Zamile : Phum ' egusheni Dikela omhle ungajikelezi .
Iingxaki zobudoda zingangoboya benja .
Thembile : Bawokazi ndifuna ukuba ndiphethuke kukho umtshakazi ojikeleza phakathi kwalo mzi
Zamile : Watsho kakuhle mfo wam .
Bendicinga ukutsho zonke ezi ntsuku koko ndisoyika ukuba nxamnye neengcina zakho .
Ngaba phofu mfo wam umi njani etikini .
Kaloku ukuzeka asikokudlala undize .
Kufuneka indoda isebenze ingafekethi ngemali .
Thembile : Kwelo cala akukho ngxaki tat'omncinci .
Imali ikhona . .
Apha ngentla uThembile uyazibika kutat'omncinci wakhe ngenjongo zakhe zokuthatha umfazi , kwaye uyamqinisekisa ukuba ume kakuhle nangasemalini , ikhazi uza kukwazi ukulibhatala akukho ngxaki .
Ingxaki iqala apho uThembile athi xa ecela ukuthatha nokuba ngamathobele ambalwa ebuhlanti , ze uZamile angavumi .
Yive le ncoko iqhubeka :
Thembile : Kwelo cala akukho ngxaki tat'omncinci .
Imali ikhona yaye ndicinga ukuba singathatha nokuba mathathu kula mathole asebuhlanti .
Zamile : Kaloku mfo wam akunakho ukucinga ngala mathole asebuhlanti xa ufuna ukuzeka .
Ziinkomo zeli khaya ezi asizizo ?
Thembile : Ewe tata andijonganga zona .
Ndijonge ukuba sibhenele kuzo xa kucaca ukuba umcimbi uyenyuka malunga nelobola .
Zamile : Sukufane ucinge ngezi nkomo , Thembile .
Loo nto ndiyayithetha andiyinkuntuzi .
Iinkomo ezi zezam .
Thembile : Kanene tat ' omncinci asinguwe na owandibonisa iinkomo ezazithengwe ngubawo esaphila ?
Zamile : Ewe ndim mfo wam , Uyihlo esaphila ndamncedisa ngamathokazi amabini ekuzekeni kwakhe ngenjongo yokuba naye uya kwenjenjalo ekuzekeni kwam .
Ngelishwa ke iNkosi yakhawuleza yamphuthuma .
Ke ezi iinkomo zikolu thango lwam
azinakho ukuphinda zibizwe ngaye .
Qokelela imali wena uze nayo ukuze sikwazi ukuqalisa umncimbi wokukuzekela .
Ndigqibile ke Qwathi .
( Atsho aphakame ayimise ngothango echitha amanzi . )
UZamile akavumanga kwaphela neenkomo zokuncedisana noThembile nangona wayekhe watsho ukuba zikho nezikatata kaThembile phakathi kwazo .
Kodwa ngoku ume ngxi ukuba uThembile akazokufumana nokuba inye kwiinkomo ezisebuhlanti .
Kodwa njengamntu uthatha indawo katata kaThembile kuba owakhe utata wasweleka , kodwa ngoku xa uThembile efuna inkxaso yakhe , uzikhupha ngaphandle .
UNojenti akayithandi tu into yokuzeka kukaThembile .
Konke oku kuye kubangelwa ngumona .
Kuvelwa ukuyokucelwa intombi ebonwe nguThembile , eyibonele ukuyitshata .
Bathi xa bebuya , bebuya nengxelo , uNojenti akakwazi ukuzibamba ngendlela anomona ngayo ngokutshata kukaThembile .
KwaZamile kuhleli uZamile , Kholisile noMdendo .
Oonozakuzaku beze nengxelo .
Zamile : Khanitsho nto zikabawo , nihambe njani ?
Mdendo : Sihambe kakuhle kakhulu mkhuluwa khange sisokoliswe tu .
Zamile : Abanibethanga kakhulu kodwa ?
Kholisile : Hayi mkhuluwa .
Bathe kratya nje kancinci ukudlula kuleya yethu iminwe .
Zamile : Yitsho kaloku .
Badlule kangakanani ?
Kholisile : Bengeze iinkomo ezintlanu ezintlanu ezinethole , baza bathi ezintathu kufuneka zihambe ngamanqina .
Nojenti : ( Eburhamla esentla ) Rhaa !
Ndingatsho nje ukuba yinkosazana le niyizekayo ?
Yakha yakho intombi elotyolwa ngeenkomo ezingakonexabso eliphezulu olo hlobo ?
Mdendo : Naso ke isimanga !
Kwakha kwanje phi na ?
Sathi sixoxa umcimbi wakwaNoni kwaNoni kwangenela umendi singammemanga , kuhle ntoni ?
Zamile : Nojenti !
Nojenti !
Nojenti !
Nceda ulungise izinto zakho phandle siza kukubiza xa sikufuna .
Nojenti : ( Ephuma ) Hayi kodwa nizizisulu .
Bonke abantu baya kuzihlolela apha kuni iintombi zabo baze bakwazi ukubiza unothanda .
Kuqala uNojenti ubonisa ubukrwada kunye nongabi nambeko ngokuthi angenelele kwincoko engamfuniyo xeshikweni kuxoxa amadoda ekhaya ngendaba zelobola kaThembile .
Ekubeni engenantlonipho enjalo , ubonisa ubukrwada ngendlela avela aphoseleke ngayo ephendula ingxoxo ekude kunaye .
Kwaye uthetha ngendlela erhabaxa ngokungathi uthetha nabahlobo bakhe .
Kwelinye icala uTeteleza noNontsipho nabo abayithandi into yokuthandana nokuzekana kukaNomava noThembile .
Bona banomona kuba benqwenela ukuba uNomava athandane , endele kuNtemese unyana kaTeteleza .
Khabave ke xa bexoxa ngalomba : Teteleza : Mholo ntokazi .
Walibala kukonwaba nkazana akuyivanga ingxaki endikuyo ?
Nontsipho : Yiza nazo Teteleza mfazi : Ndizifuna ngoku zingekabethwa yimitha yelanga .
Phokoza mfazi isifuba sam somile .
Andinayo nento entsha endiza kungena ngayo phakathi kwabanye abafazi namhlanje .
Ayilunganga into yokuya uze phakathi kwamanye amakhosikazi .
Kufuneka qho kusisa ufike nenqaku elitsha nokuba liyachitha , nokuba likhaya , ayifuni ooNontsipho loo nto .
Thina sisebenzisa izixhobo esazinikwa nguThixo .
( Atsho esalatha elulwimini )
Teteleza : Wethu !
Andilalanga phezolo ngunyana wam uNtemese .
Ubusuku bonke uyashwabula ethetha kalusizi mfazi .
Nontsipho : Uthi nansti intoni na lo mntwana , Teteleza ?
Nontsipho mfazi , uNtemee uliliswa kukubona esaa simoyoywana singuThembile sincokola ngokuzola noNomava , de baqwele ngokuphuzana xa besahlukana .
Nontsipho : Yhe Teteleza !
Uthi uyayiva le nto uyithethayo ?
Ucinga ukuba uNomava angaze abe nento ayithetha nalla mzobololo womnyewu wakwaSifuba ?
Yintoni yna laa nto , into esoloko ithe bhaku iindlebe ngathi ityiwa ngamakhalane .
Teteleza : Nontsipho !
Ikamba labantwana bethu lisezandleni zethu .
Ukunyaba kwabo kuxhomekeke kuthi .
Umntwana wam ukhathazekile .
Ukuba unalo mfazi icebo libeke etafileni .
Musa ukolula intetho ngathi uyahleka .
Kubi mfazi .
Esi sibini siyenze kwacaca gca apha kule ncoko ingentla into yokuba le ndibano kaThembile kunye noNomava abayithandisisi kwaphela kwaye bengayithandisisi nje kufuneka kwenziwe icebo lokuba iqhiwulwe .
Ngenxa yokubona le meko kaNojenti , uThembile ugqiba ekubeni ayeke ukuphangela kuba engafuni ukushiya uNomava kolunjalo uchuku .
uNojenti umphatha kakubi uNomava kuba efuna ukuba ahambe .
Izenzo zempatho mbi kaNojenti zide zimphathe kakubi uNomava , ade afune ukuhamba , le nto kanye ifunwa nguNojenti .
Mve uNomava ethetha nomnyeni wakhe ngempatho - mbi kaNojenti :
Nomava : ( Elila ) Bhuti Thembile ingathi ndazikhanda ngenyheke elityeni ukuvuma isicelo sakho .
Umama wakho akafuni nokundibona , kunjalo nje ndinoloyiko lwento eya kuzalwa yile meko ndiyibonayo .
Bhuti Thembile sithandwa sam ndilusizi ukuba ndithi ndifika kowenu ndithethe ngomzali wakho kuwe , kodwa ke nawe uyabona ukuba kufanelekile ndenze njalo .
Thembile : Kunjalo mfazi .
Umama uyawuchitha mpela lo mzi .
Kodwa yonke le nto intsha , ifikisene nokuzeka oku kwam .
Besaxoxa njalo nanku uNojenti engena nobukrwada bakhe :
Nojenti : Nkqonkqo - nkqo .
Yintoni emzini wam ndabona sendinamaxhwele ?
Yintoni ebangela ukuba ningavuki Thembile nale ntlubuntlubu yomntwana ongenambeko ?
Wena , ngaphandle kobudenge obu bakho wakha wambona umtshakazi elala kude kuphume ilanga ?
Ndifuna ukucoca indlu yam ngoku phumani phandle .
Nomava : Tyhini mama !
Kudala ndiyibona le nto yakho .
Uthi masiphume ngeli xesha ?
Kutheni le nto ungakwaziyo ukuyiquma inkohlakalo yakho ?
Nojenti : Ndaza ndasiva isimanga sokukhonkothwa ngumtshakazi okracakraca .
Yintoni le ndiyiziselwe emzini wam ?
Ndodle , ndondle inkedama kanti ndizilolela izembe .
Sokuze ndizokulawulwa emzini wam .
Nditsho ndithi phumani nakuzibonela ukuba maniyephi na .
Nomava : Utsho phantsi mama .
Mna andiyi ndawo .
Ukuba uyandigxotha kufuneka uthumele oonozakuzaku ekhaya baye kuxela ukuba babengandiceleli mzi .
Ukuba leyo iyakoyisa yitsho kwakwabo nozakuzaku bandigoduse qha ke .
Thembile : Mama yeka le nto uyenzayo .
Umona awunakamva .
Nojenti : Thula wena .
Uzibona ubudoda ngoku .
Wakha waphendula kum kakade ngokuya wawungekazeki ?
Thembile : Wawungangcungcuthekisa mna ndeda .
Andinakuthula kuba umntwana lo wabantu uze ngam apha , ke andinakubukela ephekwa esophulwa .
Nojenti : Ndokhe ndibone ukuba nakulala phi na namhlanje .
Watsho ephosa iingubo zabo nokhuko phandle .
Xa kuxoxwa , kulungiswa uchuku lukaNojenti kuvuka uthuli ngenxa yokuthukwa kukaMdendo nguNojenti .
UMdendo uqhwaba uNojenti ngempama .
UZamile ubetha uMdendo ngenduku ambulale enqandela uNonjenti .
uKholisile uqobongela uThembile ukuba bangaxeli ukuba nguZamile obulele uMdendo koko bathi ujuleke wawa , wasweleka .
Impatheko - mbi kaNomava iyenyukela .
uNomava ufumana umntwana bamthiye igama elinguMava .
UNontsipho noTeteleza beza necebo lokubulala uThembile kuNojenti naye alamkele .
UZamile ubulawa kukusela utywala obunetyhefu obebulungiselelwe uThembile .
UNojenti ukruneka isinqe xa esukela endlwini ukuya kuphazamisa uZamile angaseli utywala obunetyhefu .
UNojenti uyayichaza ityhefu ukuba uyifumene kuNontsipho noTeteleza abamelwane bakhe .
Bayakhanyela ooNontsipho noTeteleza .
Isibhedlela simnika isitulo esinamavili uNojenti kuba kucaca ukuba akanakho ukuphinda ahambe ngeenyawo zakhe .
UNojenti ucela uxolo " Ndixoleleni " kuNovanya , Thembile , Nomava nakuwo onke amaQwathi ngokuwuvunduza awuchithachithe umzi ngochuku nomona .
Ndaba nomona kukuzeka kukaThembile , ndimmonela ngayo yonke into eniyibonayo kulo mzi .
Ndamtshutshisa ndimngcungcuthekamisa nomfazi wakhe ndicinga ukuba uya kukruquka ahambe koko wanyamezela .
Ubhuti uMdendo wabulaliswa ndim kuba indoda yam yayinqanda mna emva kokuba ndimthukile .
Indoda yam yabulawa ndim kuba ndandingbafuni abantu bomzi wam apha kulo mzi .
Ityhefu eyabulalaumyeni wam ndandiyinikwe nguTeteleza noNontsipho .
Namhlanje andikwazi kuhamba ndilusana .
Ndixoleleni nonke .
Ndicela uxolo Nomava .
Uze uncede undigcine mntwana wam ndikubonile ukunyamezelakwakho .
Yonke into elapha kulo mzi endandikumonela ngayo , namhlanje ndiyinika wena noThembile .
Elo lifa ulinikwe nguThixa ngenxa yokunyamezela kwakho .
UNojenti ude wazibona iziphumo zezenzo zakhe wabona ukuba ulenzile udushe olukhulu nobubi obungaphaya kokuqonda .
Ngoku ucela uxolo kubo bonke abo athe wabona ngoba uyabona ukuba uqol'uphandle ngoku .
Uyazivuma zonke izono zakhe , kwaye uyavuma ngoku into yokuba zonke izenzo zakhe besikhokelwa lumona .
Zonke izinto zakhe uzinikela kuThembile noNomava .
Bonke bayamxolela .
uNonjenti UKholisile uxhela inkabi yenkomo ukubulela uThixo nezinyanya ngokuphinda abuyisele uxolo nobunye kumzi wakwaSifuba .
Nomava : Musa ukulila mama , sula iinyembezi .
Mna noThembile sakuxolela kudala , sokuze sikulahle .
Novanya : Nam ndimxolele kuba siyafana .
Naye ungumhlolokazi kodwa yena ungcono kuba nguye ozibeke kuloo ndawo .
Nojenti : NguNontsipho noTeteleza zinkosi zam .
Owu !
Nandenza zihlobo zam zabumini .
Akhale kwakhona , Ndixoleleni .
Ndixoleleni .
Kholisile : ( Ebhekisa kuThembile ) Mfo wam umvile unyoko ezisola ecela uxolo kananjalo .
Le nto yenzekileyo asikokuthanda kwamntu .
Yintando kaThixo afuna ngayo ukuzibonakalisa ubukhulu bakhe .
Uze uncede ungabi nanqala kunyoko amile ngezinto abazenza nabazithetha kuwe .
Ndiyaphinda ndithi uze ungabanqali abazali bakho .
Ngabazali bakho aba kuba bakondlile bakukhulisa wada waba yile ndoda uyiyo .
Yonke le nto yenzekileyo uze ungayibambi . . .
Ukuhlamba eli lishwa lokuchithakala komzi , ngomso ndifuna kuhlatywe laa nkabi yenkomo imnyama yam sitye sonke nelali ize kungqina xa sibulela uThixo ngokuphinda avuselele uxolo nobunye phakathi kosapho lwakwaSifuba .
Nanko ke uNojenti ezisola ngezenzo zakhe zokungcola .
Ngelaka nethamsanqa , wone abantu abanobuntu kunye noekibuThixo , abakwaziyo ukuxola xa bebona ukuba umntu ebelahlekile .
Bona ooThembile nooKholisile abenzi le nto yayisenziwa nguNojenti yokuvalela abantu ngaphandle engafuni nokuba bona , bona bayalamkela uxolo lwakhe ngentliziyo ezikhululekileyo ngoba bayaqonda ukuba umona yinto apha enobungozi , kwaye etshabalalisayo .
Makuthenjwe ke ukuba uNojenti usifundile isifunde sakhe , kwaye uyaqonda ngoku into yokuba , umona alwakhi .
Ukuba luyalandeleka kakuhle olu phando , kuya kukhumbuleka ukuba pha ekuqaleni kwintshayelelo bekukhankanyiwe ukuba , eli icandelo lijonga indlela ababhali besini sobuduna abathi bazibhalo ngalo izibhalo zabo zedrama kunye nendlela ababazoba ngayo abalinganiswa babo abangamabhinqa .
Unobangela wokuba oku kukhankanywe kwakhona kungenxa yokuthungelana kweli bali u - " Ndixoleleni " kunye neliya lithi , " Inene Nasi Isibhozo . "
Xa sijonga eli ibali le drama , kuye kubonakale ngokucacileyo ukufana phakathi kwawo kunye neliya likaMtingane .
Omakaqapheleke kukuba bobabini aba babhali babhale ezi ncwadi zedrama ngabantu besilisa , kwaye indlela ababazoba ngayo abalinganiswa babo ababhinqileyo ifana nkcakasa .
Kwa umxholo wala mabali mabini uyafana .
Yiyo loo nto umphandi ezikhethe zombini ezi ncwadi ukubonisa into yokuba ababhali besilisa babazoba ngokufanayo abalinganiswa abangamabhiqa .
Nakweli bali umba obalaseleyo bubugqwirha nokukhohlakala kwamabhinqa , anamona kwaye aqhutywa kukungcola kwizenzo zabo .
Oku sikubona kwiintshukumo zomlinganiswa obhinqileyo uNonjenti .
Kodwa ke olu phando luza kungena nzulu koku , ze luveze banzi oku kuthethwa ngako , kujongwe aba balinganiswa bazotywe ngokufanayo kwelinye ibali ebeselikhankanyiwe .
Umlinganiswa oyintloko kweli bali kungatshiwo ukuba nguMasukude .
Uthe akuswelekelwa ngumyeni wakhe uNjinge , waye washiyeka nonyana wakhe uVuma , kwaze kwathi kokuhamba ixesha , wafikelela kwelokuba unyana wakhe uVuma makazekelwe umfazi ngoba ke kaloku yena ufuna umntu oza kujongana nekhaya , ancedisane naye kwimisebenzi yaphakathi ekhayeni ngoba yena uyaguga , kwaye naye uVuma
uye esiba mdala .
Kodwa ukubuya kukaThemba eKapa kwazimosha zonke iinzame zikaMasukude ngokuba kaloku bekungasokuze kukwazi ukuzekelwe uVuma , abe umkhuluwa wakhe yena engekazekelwa .
Elo ke lisiko lakwaXhosa , ngoko ke bekungekho ndlela yokuba uMasukude aphikisane naloo nto , ngoba isiko aliphikiswa liyahlonelwa .
UMasukude wabonakala kwasekuqaleni ukuba uzakuba yingxaki kulo mzi , kuba kuhleliinje kukhalwa ngesimilo sakhe , nendlela angakwazi ngayo ukuziphatha .
Yiyo lo nto abaninawa nabakhuluwa omnyeni wakhe ongasekhoyo baqonda izinto zomzi kabhuti wabo bazithathele kuba , hayi bayiyekele kuMasukude ongevayo oko mntwana ongaqeqeshekanga .
Mve omnye wabo eyicacisa le nto : Mfolo : ( KuLolo ) Khawume kuhle ( KuMasukude ) Uyabona Masukude kukwaNjinge ekhay'apha .
Lo ngumzi waseMakhwalweni .
Okoko kwabhubha uNjinge , lomzi waba ngundaba - mlonyeni phakathi kwezivondoviya zochuku ezikhoyo kule lali .
Namhlanje ulwa noMadlamini ngento engekhoyo .
Nisakuba nilanyulwe , usuka uye kubaqhiwulela ethafeni .
Nalapho usokoyiswa , ufunza uVuma ukuba aye kubetha ooninamncinci .
Nantsi into emandikuphe yona : Kusekho uNjinge , besiyichitha imini sonwabile ekhay'apha , simke kungekabikho kukrwentsa - krwentsana ; kodwa ngoku sibetha emva kwezindlu ngenxa yesimilo sakho osiphethe ngezandla .
Kanti ke , khumbula ukuba indoda yakho iyazibona zonke ezi zinto zingamasikizi uzenzayo .
Thina ke bakowayo asinakukukhalala kuphele kuba sakuba sikhalala yona .
Nanku uLolo , umninawe kaNjinge , oliliso lalo mzi .
Ukuba kukho into ekuxakileyo okanye ongayithandiyo , yibike kuye nibonisane ngayo nobabini .
Andifuni kuphinda ndithethe ngolu hloboo kuwe .
Xa ndize ekhaya apha , ndingavuya ndize umzimba wam ukhululekile , ndifike wonke wonke umntu onwabile , nam ndibuye ndimke kusahlekwa .
Qweba isimilo ke njengawo onke amakhosikazi andilekileyo .
Esi similo sikaMasukude sobubi sibonwe kwakude kudala , seqhanqalaze nje ekuhambeni kwencwadi , esenza ububi , ukwenza oko sekukudala wacelwa ukuba aqeqeshe isimilo sakhe .
Siyabona apha exelelwa ukuba uLolo uzakuba liliso losemzini wakhe , aze athi ancedisane naye kwizigqibo ekufuneka ezenzile phakathi kwekhaya kuba uNjinge engesakhoyo .
Kodwa yena uMasukude ufuna ukuba ngumfazi noyihloko emzini wakhe , hayi le nto yokuba kufuneka agqibe kubantu basemzini wakhe xa efuna ukuthatha isigqibo kwinto afuna ukuyenza .
Ingxwabangxwaba paya yaqala ekubeni uLolo , umninawa kaNjinge , abe kanti ujongene nalo mzi , nto ethetha ukuba nguye oza kuthi enze izigqibo zeli khaya , nto apha angayithanga kwaphela uMasukude ngoba ke kaloku , lo mzi ngowakhe , ngoke ke nguye ekumele ukuba abe yintloko .
Ekubeni uMasukude exelele uLolo ngenjongo zakhe zokuba kuzekelwe uVuma kuqala kunoThemba , uLolo uye wabiza amanye amadoda akwaNjinge ukuba kuxowe lo mba .
Kule ngxoxo uMasukude ugxothiwe ngelithi , bona abasoze baxoxe nomfazi .
Kaloku ingcingane yesini sobukhomokazi isixelela ukuba amadoda awababoni ebalulekile amabhinqa kwaye awafuni ukuwabandakanya kwizinto ezibalulekileyo zekhaya , ngelithi ngumsebenzi wobudoda lowo ngaphandleni xa esekhitshini epheka , apho indawo yabo ikhona , yiyo loo nto la madoda engakhange avume ukuba kuxoxwe phambi kukaMasukude
nje .
Iva la madoda akwaNjinge , ebhekisa kuMasukude :
UMfolo : Kuhle , ndingakuxholi , usemile njalo , ngaba lityala eli okanye sihlangene ngomcimbi wekhaya , apha kulo mzi namhlanje ?
ULolo : Sihlanene ngomcimbi wekhaya .
UMfolo : Ngaba imicimbi yomzi apha siyixoxa kunye nabafazi ?
ULolo : Asiyilungisi nabafazi .
UMfolo : Lo ke umfazi uza kwaneka umcimbi womzi emadodeni , uza kusanekela ngabuni ?
UMfolo : Wethu , mus " undiyilozela .
Asinguwe na iliso lalo mzi akubhubha umkhuluwa wakho ?
UMazwazwa : Unyanisile umkhuluwa lo .
Usisi unokubizwa sithi xa kukh " into esifuna ukuyiqonda .
UMfolo : ( Ekhomba uLolo ) khangela ndiyakunyola ngoku .
Xa axoxayo ke amadoda , aphikisana de anyolane .
Uthi ke wena uMasukude makanyolane noyisezala kunye nabakhuluwa bakhe apha ?
Tyhini , bafondini , Ngooban'aba baza kubhenguzelwa ngeelokhwe ?
( kuMasukude ) Masukude , thatha i - emele uyokukha amanzi , upheke , sakukubiza xa sikufuna .
Umzizi : Ngokwenyaniso epheleleyo , asimelwe kukuphikisana noMasukude xa sixoxa .
Buyimpazama ubukho bakhe .
Kambe nakuthi kuyimpazamo ukukrazula xa sithetha kukho umntu obhinqileyo ; kaloku bakhathazeka msinya yintetho eqatha nerhabaxa .
Ezi ntetho zivela kula madoda athetha apha ngentla , zingaphikiswa mpela ngamabhinqa alwela ukulingana phakathi kwamadoda namabhinqa .
Ngoba kaloku la madoda athetha ukuba abafazi abanawo amandla okuxoxa izinto ezibalulekileyo kwaye ezinzima .
Nto apha ekhatywayo ngala mabhinqa , ngoba afuna ukubonisa amadoda into yokuba nawo anako ukumelana neengxoko zekhaya , yiyo loo nto zifuna ukubandakanywa xa kusenziwa iingxoxo ezilolu hlobo .
Yiyo loo nto ingakhange ingene kamnandi kuMasukude into yokuba izinto zomzi wakhe zixoxwe ngaphandle kwakhe .
Ibe ibubomi bonyana wakhe wokuqala nowokugqibela lo kuxoxwa ngaye .
Noko ngebemvumele ukuba ahlale amamele nokuba ke abamvumelanga ukuba ahlomle .
Umxholo weli bali kungatshiwo ukuba kukubaluleka kokuhlonipha nokuthobela isiko ngoba ingxaki iqale xa uMasukude efuna ukutshintsha isiko ukuze izinto zenzeke ngolwakhe uhlobo .
